prepared.module target=riscv64-linux-gnu route=semantic_bir_shared
completed_phases: legalize stack_layout liveness out_of_ssa regalloc
invariants:
  - no_target_facing_i1
  - no_phi_nodes
notes:
  - [prealloc] prealloc owns the shared semantic-BIR to prealloc-BIR route before MIR lowering
  - [legalize] bootstrap BIR legalize kept semantic CFG and phi form intact while promoting i1 values plus function signature/storage bookkeeping, memory-address/load-store bookkeeping, and call ABI metadata
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'PrintAll' with 1 home slot(s) and 4 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'Move' with 8 home slot(s) and 32 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'Hanoi' with 0 home slot(s) and 0 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'main' with 1 home slot(s) and 4 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout now emits provisional stack objects, elides dead and copy-coalesced home slots, and only allocates frame storage for objects that still require dedicated homes
  - [liveness] liveness now computes BIR named-value intervals, exact def/use program points, predecessor-edge phi uses, call points, CFG-aware live-through extension, and loop depth independently of stack-layout object identity
  - [out_of_ssa] out_of_ssa removed phi nodes from live prepared BIR and published authoritative join-transfer plus parallel-copy obligations
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'PrintAll' with 55 allocation constraint(s) and 289 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 21 register(s) and 34 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'Move' with 46 allocation constraint(s) and 134 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 18 register(s) and 28 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'Hanoi' with 9 allocation constraint(s) and 26 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 7 register(s) and 2 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'main' with 53 allocation constraint(s) and 353 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 14 register(s) and 39 stack slot(s)

bir.func @Move(ptr %p.source, ptr %p.dest) -> i32 {
entry:
  bir.store_local %lv.i, i32 0
  bir.store_local %lv.j, i32 0
  bir.br block_14
block_14:
  %t0 = bir.load_local i32 %lv.i
  %t1 = bir.slt i32 %t0, 4
  bir.cond_br i32 %t1, logic.rhs.4, logic.skip.5
logic.rhs.4:

bir.func @Hanoi(i32 %p.n, ptr %p.source, ptr %p.dest, ptr %p.spare) -> void {

  bir.call void Hanoi(i32 %t4, ptr %p.source, ptr %p.spare, ptr %p.dest)
  ; call_arg_source index=0 encoding=register source_value_id=107 source_value=%t4

  ; call_arg_source index=2 encoding=computed_address source_value=%p.spare source_base=%p.spare source_delta=0
  ; call_arg_source index=3 encoding=computed_address source_value=%p.dest source_base=%p.dest source_delta=0

  ; call_arg_source index=1 encoding=computed_address source_value=%p.dest source_base=%p.dest source_delta=0
  %t6 = bir.sub i32 %p.n, 1

  ; call_arg_source index=0 encoding=register source_value_id=109 source_value=%t6
